namespace = ngm_tradition
# 大規模建築計画局
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.1
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		# add_research_option = tech_mega_engineering
		add_tech_progress = {
			tech = tech_mega_engineering
			progress = 0.5
		}
	}
}

# 研鑽(自らを磨き、高みへと目指すことこそが求められる)
# 3.資格採用の強化:リーダー初期レベル+1
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.3
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_program_study
	}
	immediate = {
		every_owned_leader = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_leader_flag = flag_tr_ngm_program_study
				}
			}
			set_leader_flag = flag_tr_ngm_program_study
			add_experience = 200
		}
	}
}

# 前衛(新たな試みと反秩序こそ自己を表現することができる)
# 完遂時:取得している国是をすべて削除する

# 狙い撃ち:艦船連射レート+5%、宿敵の犯罪度+10		伝統取得時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.5
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_sniper
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
					has_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
			set_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
			every_rival_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
					days = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_ngm_virture_rival_country_1
				}
				event_target:ngm_virture_rival_country_1 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
							}
						}
						add_modifier = {
							modifier = tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
							days = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_ngm_virture_rival_country_2
				}
				event_target:ngm_virture_rival_country_2 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
							}
						}
						add_modifier = {
							modifier = tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
							days = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_ngm_virture_rival_country_3
				}
				event_target:ngm_virture_rival_country_3 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
							}
						}
						add_modifier = {
							modifier = tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
							days = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {

# 狙い撃ち:宿敵の犯罪度+30		月ごとのチェック
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.6
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_sniper
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
			}
			every_rival_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					days = 30
					modifier = tr_ngm_sniper_debuff_1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_ngm_virture_rival_country_1
				}
				event_target:ngm_virture_rival_country_1 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {

country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.7
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_penetration

# 浸透:外交関係にあるすべての国家の犯罪度+20		月ごとのチェック
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.8
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_penetration
	}
	immediate = {
		every_playable_country = {
			limit = {
				has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_1
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_2
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_3
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_4
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_4
			}

				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_penetration_debuff_5
				}

# 破壊工作:宿敵の貿易保護値-15、宿敵の犯罪度+20		伝統取得時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.11
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_sabotage
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_1
					has_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_1
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_1
			set_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_1
			every_rival_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_1
					days = 30
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_ngm_virture_rival_country_1
				}
				event_target:ngm_virture_rival_country_1 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
							}
						}

							modifier = tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_1

							modifier = tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_8
							days = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = country_flag_ngm_virture_rival_country_16
				}
				event_target:ngm_virture_rival_country_16 = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
							}
						}
						add_modifier = {
							modifier = tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_8
							days = 30
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# every_rival_country = {
			# 	limit = {
			# 		has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
			# 	}
			# 	remove_modifier = tr_ngm_sabotage_debuff_8

# 恒常的妨害:宿敵の貿易保護値-5		伝統取得時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.1011
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_constant_obstruction
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_constant_obstruction_debuff_1
					has_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_constant_obstruction_debuff_1
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_constant_obstruction_debuff_1
			set_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_constant_obstruction_debuff_1
			every_rival_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = tr_ngm_constant_obstruction_debuff_1
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}

					has_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_constant_obstruction_debuff_2

# 国家宣伝省:宿敵1つあたりの影響力収入+1		伝統取得時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.13
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 1
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 2
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 3
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 5
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
			}
		}
	}
}

# 国家宣伝省:宿敵1つあたりの影響力収入+1		月ごとのチェック
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.14
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 1
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 2
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 3
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_3
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				num_rivals = 5
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_2

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
				}
				remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministry_engagement_buff_4
			}
		}
	}

# 善隣完遂時:5種類以上の種族がいる惑星でPop成長速度+10%、交易価値+10%、統合力+10%、流入魅力+10%		伝統取得時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.15
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_neighbor_finish
	}
	immediate = {
		every_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				num_species >= 5
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_neighbor_finish_buff
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ngm_tradition.18
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_military_police
	}
	immediate = {
		every_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				num_armies >= 10
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_military_police_buff
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_military_police_buff
			}
		}
		every_owned_planet = {
			limit = {
				num_armies < 10
				has_modifier = tr_ngm_military_police_buff
			}
			remove_modifier = tr_ngm_military_police_buff
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.25
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_constant_hostile_intelligence_operations
	}
	immediate = {

			set_global_flag = global_flag_ap_ngm_chio_debuff_1
			set_country_flag = country_flag_ap_ngm_chio_debuff_1

# 宗主取得時:忠誠度月間+1		伝統取得時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.27
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_suzerain_finish
	}
	immediate = {
		every_subject = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_suzerain_adopt_modifier
			}
		}
	}
}

# 宗主取得時:忠誠度月間+1		月ごとチェック
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.28
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_suzerain_finish
	}
	immediate = {
		every_subject = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerain_adopt_modifier
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = tr_ngm_suzerain_adopt_modifier
			}
		}
	}
}

# 宗主取得時:忠誠度月間+1		解除月ごとチェック
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.29
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			is_subject = no
			has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
		}
		OR = {
			has_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerain_adopt_modifier
			has_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerainty_pressure_modifier
			has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministory_culture_modifier
			has_modifier = civic_ngm_missionary_group_modifier
			has_modifier = ap_ngm_dipromatic_think_tank_modifier
			has_modifier = ap_ngm_layer_countries_modifier
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerain_adopt_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerain_adopt_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerainty_pressure_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = tr_ngm_suzerainty_pressure_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = tr_ngm_ministory_culture_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = tr_ngm_ministory_culture_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = civic_ngm_missionary_group_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = civic_ngm_missionary_group_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = ap_ngm_dipromatic_think_tank_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = ap_ngm_dipromatic_think_tank_modifier
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_modifier = ap_ngm_layer_countries_modifier
			}
			remove_modifier = ap_ngm_layer_countries_modifier
		}
	}
}

# 40.芸術外交:月間忠誠度+1	伝統取得時 	237.領地相続:毎月の忠誠心+1
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.32
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_tradition = tr_ngm_diplomatic_art
			has_tradition = tr_ngm_territory_inheritance
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tradition = tr_ngm_diplomatic_art
			}
			every_subject = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = tr_ngm_ministory_culture_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tradition = tr_ngm_territory_inheritance
			}
			every_subject = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = tr_ngm_territory_inheritance_modifier
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# 40.芸術外交:月間忠誠度+1		月ごとチェック

# 84.敵対的演説:宿敵の外交発言力-10%
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.34
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_battle_speach
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_1
					has_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_1
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_1
			set_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_1
			every_rival_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					modifier = tr_ngm_battle_speach_modifier_1
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOR = {
					has_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_2
					has_country_flag = country_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_2
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = global_flag_tr_ngm_battle_speach_2

# 2.外交シンクタンク	外交官+2 外交発言力+20% 月間忠誠度+1
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.36
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_dipromatic_think_tank
	}
	immediate = {
		every_subject = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_ascension_perk = ap_ngm_ministry_of_innocence
				}
			}
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = ap_ngm_dipromatic_think_tank_modifier
			}
		}
	}
}

# 前衛(新たな試みと反秩序こそ自己を表現することができる)
# 完遂時:国是を削除分追加分岐
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.40
	title = ngm_tradition.40.name
	desc = ngm_tradition.40.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_announcement
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = tr_ngm_avantgarde_finish_variable
			value > 0
		}
	}
	# バニラ通常帝国用国是
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.41
			}
		}
	}
	# バニラ企業帝国用国是
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.57
			}
		}
	}
	# バニラ集合意識
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.c
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.50
			}
		}
	}
	# バニラ機械集合意識
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.d
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.53
			}
		}
	}
	# 追加通常帝国用国是
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.e
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.61
			}
		}
	}
	# 追加企業帝国用国是
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.f
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.91
			}
		}
	}
	# 閉じる
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.40.g
	}
}

# 完遂時:国是を削除分追加1 バニラ通常帝国用国是
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.41
	title = ngm_tradition.41.name
	desc = ngm_tradition.41.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_announcement
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = tr_ngm_avantgarde_finish_variable
			value > 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.41.a
		allow = {
			NOT = {
				has_ethic = ethic_gestalt_consciousness
			}
			NOT = {
				has_authority = auth_corporate
			}
			NOR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			}
			NOT = {
				has_civic = civic_free_haven
			}
			NOT = {
				has_civic = civic_corvee_system
			}
		}

country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.91
	title = ngm_tradition.41.name
	desc = ngm_tradition.41.desc
	picture = GFX_evt_announcement
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		check_variable = {
			which = tr_ngm_avantgarde_finish_variable
			value > 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.91.a
		allow = {
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_honorism
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_honorism
			}
			has_authority = auth_corporate
			NOT = {
				has_civic = civic_ngm_corporate_empire
			}
		}
		force_add_civic = civic_ngm_corporate_empire
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = tr_ngm_avantgarde_finish_variable
				value = 1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ngm_tradition.40
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ngm_tradition.91.b
		allow = {
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
			has_authority = auth_corporate
			NOT = {
				has_civic = civic_ngm_high_tech_company
			}

				which = tr_ngm_avantgarde_finish_variable

			}

				id = ngm_tradition.40
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_developmentalism
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_developmentalism

			has_authority = auth_corporate
			NOR = {
				has_civic = civic_ngm_high_tech_company
				has_civic = civic_ngm_hereditary_officers
				has_civic = civic_ngm_financial_enterprises
				has_civic = civic_ngm_information_company
				has_civic = civic_ngm_social_enterprise
			}
			NOT = {

# 逆境 完遂時:防衛戦争時に亜高速移動速度+20% 開始時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.1001
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_adversity_finish
		is_at_war = yes
		any_war = {
			any_defender = {
				is_same_value = prevprev
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		add_modifier = {
			modifier = tr_ngm_adversity_finish_modifier
		}
	}
}

# 逆境 完遂時:防衛戦争時に亜高速移動速度+20% 終了時
country_event = {
	id = ngm_tradition.1002
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_tradition = tr_ngm_adversity_finish
		is_at_war = yes
		any_war = {
			any_defender = {
				is_same_value = prevprev
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		remove_modifier = tr_ngm_adversity_finish_modifier
	}
}
